introduced the first Aimpoint red dot optic to the market in 1975. &nbsp;Since then, Aimpoint continues to innovate.&nbsp;</p> <p>Many competitors have tried to duplicate the Aimpoint scope, but they all fall short in terms of reliability and durability. &nbsp;While there are lower priced products on the market, we like Aimpoint; not only for their ruggedness but for how well they perform in the field. &nbsp;It's obvious to see you're holding a quality built product when you hold an Aimpoint.&nbsp;</p> <p>Our company started selling Aimpoint optics back in 1996 when we first started the company. &nbsp;We continue to feature and recommend Aimpoint as one of our premier optics brands to our customers. &nbsp;We have rarely seen a disappointed customer or any problems with the products being returned. &nbsp;We see this as a testament to customer satisfaction. &nbsp;<br>Aimpoint scopes are engineered to withstand abuse under harsh conditions. &nbsp; They feature parallax-free,
